                        <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 1200 600" data-related-device="desktopPortrait" class="n2-ow n2-ss-preserve-size n2-ss-preserve-size--slider n2-ss-slide-limiter"></svg><div data-first="1" data-slide-duration="0" data-id="28" data-slide-public-id="1" data-title="Slide 1" class="n2-ss-slide n2-ow  n2-ss-slide-28"><div role="note" class="n2-ss-slide--focus" tabindex="-1">Slide 1</div><div class="n2-ss-layers-container n2-ss-slide-limiter n2-ow"><div class="n2-ss-layer n2-ow n-uc-1RXesF1jPTqE" data-sstype="slide" data-pm="default"><div class="n2-ss-layer n2-ow n-uc-16610d53ccff8" data-pm="default" data-sstype="content" data-hasbackground="0"><div class="n2-ss-section-main-content n2-ss-layer-with-background n2-ss-layer-content n2-ow n-uc-16610d53ccff8-inner"><div class="n2-ss-layer n2-ow n-uc-r0XyMsKvqoVN" data-pm="normal" data-sstype="layer"><div id="n2-ss-4item1" class="n2-font-7e4b22a176b6c268c1fa27f5fcb6e8b5-hover   n2-ss-item-content n2-ss-text n2-ow" style="display:block;">Grand Libraries</div></div><div class="n2-ss-layer n2-ow n-uc-e0eGYuJNDCpv" data-pm="normal" data-sstype="layer"><div class="n2-ss-item-content n2-ss-text n2-ow-all"><div class=""><p class="n2-font-82a0e4cd5576a783f145179a3cccd539-paragraph   ">Multiple libraries stocking lakhs of books and e-books catering to different colleges inside the campus. The Central Library is the soul of Uttaranchal University with a carpet area of 2,430 Sqm. It holds a hybrid collection of printed as well electronic resources, which include books, journals, theses dissertations databases, audio-visuals, CDs/DVDs, e-books, e-journals, reports, case studies, conference proceedings, training manuals pertaining to all subjects under various courses.</p>
</div></div></div><div class="n2-ss-layer n2-ow n-uc-18069023cf27c n2-ss-layer--auto" data-pm="normal" data-sstype="layer"><div class="n2-ss-button-container n2-ss-item-content n2-ow n2-font-e664dae274c8ca83fd9d87b19821c56b-link  n2-ss-nowrap n2-ss-button-container--non-full-width"><a class="n2-style-9bcc0be757afaf78930c2a94b7fbb220-heading  n2-ow " onclick="return false;" href="#"><div><div>Know More</div></div></a></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div data-slide-duration="0" data-id="29" data-slide-public-id="2" data-title="Slide 2" class="n2-ss-slide n2-ow  n2-ss-slide-29"><div role="note" class="n2-ss-slide--focus" tabindex="-1">Slide 2</div><div class="n2-ss-layers-container n2-ss-slide-limiter n2-ow"><div class="n2-ss-layer n2-ow n-uc-V7mmRBAag8jC" data-sstype="slide" data-pm="default"><div class="n2-ss-layer n2-ow n-uc-1bc3fe1320016" data-pm="default" data-sstype="content" data-hasbackground="0"><div class="n2-ss-section-main-content n2-ss-layer-with-background n2-ss-layer-content n2-ow n-uc-1bc3fe1320016-inner"><div class="n2-ss-layer n2-ow n-uc-jGxX8pNXbcUG" data-pm="normal" data-sstype="layer"><div id="n2-ss-4item4" class="n2-font-7e4b22a176b6c268c1fa27f5fcb6e8b5-hover   n2-ss-item-content n2-ss-text n2-ow" style="display:block;">World-class Computer Centre</div></div><div class="n2-ss-layer n2-ow n-uc-Wr3HIxjpFheS" data-pm="normal" data-sstype="layer"><div class="n2-ss-item-content n2-ss-text n2-ow-all"><div class=""><p class="n2-font-82a0e4cd5576a783f145179a3cccd539-paragraph   ">The centre supports an institute-wide 1,000 Mbps fibre optic network that connects all the academic departments, hostels, libraries, other blocks, and other central facilities to this centre. It has a computer system with servers (Linux server, domain server, database server, Thin Client Server, backup server, ERP server and storage).<br />
The e-campus comprises internet, which remains open 24 hours a day, 365 days a year and has been connected with a 1 GBPS which offers high speed and uninterrupted connectivity.</p>
</div></div></div><div class="n2-ss-layer n2-ow n-uc-Qwyl0D4WeaNy n2-ss-layer--auto" data-pm="normal" data-sstype="layer"><div class="n2-ss-button-container n2-ss-item-content n2-ow n2-font-e664dae274c8ca83fd9d87b19821c56b-link  n2-ss-nowrap n2-ss-button-container--non-full-width"><a class="n2-style-9bcc0be757afaf78930c2a94b7fbb220-heading  n2-ow " onclick="return false;" href="#"><div><div>Know More</div></div></a></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div data-slide-duration="0" data-id="30" data-slide-public-id="3" data-title="Slide 3" class="n2-ss-slide n2-ow  n2-ss-slide-30"><div role="note" class="n2-ss-slide--focus" tabindex="-1">Slide 3</div><div class="n2-ss-layers-container n2-ss-slide-limiter n2-ow"><div class="n2-ss-layer n2-ow n-uc-q33noI8AP78N" data-sstype="slide" data-pm="default"><div class="n2-ss-layer n2-ow n-uc-1cf1a6df0ba9b" data-pm="default" data-sstype="content" data-hasbackground="0"><div class="n2-ss-section-main-content n2-ss-layer-with-background n2-ss-layer-content n2-ow n-uc-1cf1a6df0ba9b-inner"><div class="n2-ss-layer n2-ow n-uc-148a3b561103d" data-pm="normal" data-sstype="layer"><div id="n2-ss-4item7" class="n2-font-7e4b22a176b6c268c1fa27f5fcb6e8b5-hover   n2-ss-item-content n2-ss-text n2-ow" style="display:block;">Auditorium</div></div><div class="n2-ss-layer n2-ow n-uc-14f82da31e86d" data-pm="normal" data-sstype="layer"><div class="n2-ss-item-content n2-ss-text n2-ow-all"><div class=""><p class="n2-font-82a0e4cd5576a783f145179a3cccd539-paragraph   ">Uttaranchal University houses Swami Vivekananda Auditorium with a seating capacity of 1,200; it also incorporates other state-of-the-art features.</p>

The hostels are equipped with all the facilities to provide a comfortable stay to students. There is provision for single room occupancy, double room occupancy, three-room occupancy, and four-room occupancy. The rooms of our hostels are well-furnished and properly lighted. Each room is furnished with a bed, mattress, study table, chair, and cupboard.</p>

The mess staff takes special care to plan out a weekly menu that satisfies the vegetarian and non-vegetarian tastes. There is a separate mess for boys and girls.</p>
